If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\\n46: // If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\\n47: // (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\\n48: // later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\\n49: // WithRateLimiter option to Events().\\n50: //\\n51: // The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\\n52: // has been made to Events() or Store().\\n53: type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\\n54: \\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\\n55: \\t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\\n56: \\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\\n57: \\n58: \\t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\\n59: \\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\\n60: \\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\\n61: \\t//\\n62: \\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\\n63: \\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\\n64: \\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\\n65: \\t//\\n66: \\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\\n67: \\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\\n68: \\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\\n69: \\t// updates:\\n70: \\t//\\n71: \\t//\\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\\n72: \\t//\\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\\n73: \\t//\\n74: \\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\\n75: \\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\\n76: \\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\\n77: \\t// sent to the observer.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\\n80: \\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\\n81: \\t// will requeue.\\n82: \\t//\\n83: \\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\\n84: \\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\\n85: \\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\\n86: \\t//\\n87: \\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\\n88: \\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\\n89: \\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\\n90: \\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\\n91: \\n92: \\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. Blocks until\\n93: \\t// the store has been synchronized or the context cancelled.\\n94: \\t// Returns a non-nil error if context is cancelled or the resource\\n95: \\t// has been stopped before store has synchronized.\\n96: \\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\\n97: }\\n98: \\n99: // New creates a new Resource[T]. Use with hive.Provide:\\n100: //\\n101: //\\tvar exampleCell = hive.Module(\\n102: //\\t\\t\\\"example\\\",\\n103: //\\t \\tcell.Provide(\\n104: //\\t\\t \\t// Provide `Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]` to \\t\\tonPodEvent(ev)\\n119: //\\t\\t   \\t}\\n120: //\\t\\t}\\n121: //\\t\\treturn e\\n122: //\\t}\\n123: //\\tfunc onPodEvent(event resource.Event[*slim_core.Pod]) {\\n124: //\\t\\tswitch event.Kind {\\n125: //\\t\\tcase resource.Sync:\\n126: //\\t\\t\\t// Pods have now been synced and the set of Upsert events\\n127: //\\t\\t\\t// received thus far forms a coherent snapshot.\\n128: //\\n129: Returns error if quota exceeded\n  - Returns nil if quota available or unlimited\n\n- `onPolicyUpsert()`: Internal handler for policy additions\n- `onPolicyDelete()`: Internal handler for policy removals\n- `GetPolicyCount()`: Helper to retrieve current count for a namespace\n\n**Thread Safety**: Uses sync.RWMutex to protect the policyCounts map from concurrent access\n\n### 4. `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`\n**Purpose**: Comprehensive test suite for PolicyQuotaController\n\n**Test Coverage**:\n- `TestPolicyQuotaControllerCheckQuota()`: Tests quota enforcement logic\n  -
